# This file contains frequent German surnames for usage with NEEX 2.0
# (Actions -> Prepare Data Set -> Replace Named Entities 2.0) only. 
# NEEX 2.0 can only process single-token surnames which do not contain 
# blank spaces. Surnames are processed case-sensitively. Hence, the
# first surname 'Schöppe' will not match the term 'schöppe'. Do not in-
# clude multi-token surnames consisting of multiple surnames such as 
# 'Schöppe-Rocher', because they will be extracted automatically.
